</header><div class="entry-content"><input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"/><p><img alt="Two hearty servings of Creamy Vegetable Risotto in dinner bowls with a side of vegan parmesan" class="aligncenter wp-image-30958 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Creamy Vegetable Risotto (30 Minutes!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-9-copy.jpg" data-pin-description="8-ingredient, 30-minute CREAMY Vegetable Risotto! Flavorful, cheesy, SO delicious #vegan #glutenfree #risotto #plantbased #minimalistbaker" data-pin-media="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/MB-Creamy-Vegetable-Risotto-Pinterest.jpg" data-pin-title="Creamy Vegetable Risotto (30 Minutes!)" height="2148" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-9-copy.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-9-copy.jpg 1432w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-9-copy-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-9-copy-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-9-copy-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-9-copy-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-9-copy-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1432"/></p>
<p>When we traveled to <a href="https://www.instagram.com/p/BZeK9mBgPSo/?taken-by=danainreallife" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Portugal</a> last year, we ate <em>so</em> much good food.</p>
<p>One of the dishes was a vegetable risotto the restaurant was able to make vegan-friendly by omitting the cheese and butter. Perhaps a cardinal sin in making risotto, but they obliged. One bite in and recipe inspiration was born.</p>
<p><img alt="Wood serving platter displaying broccolini, shallots, parsley, red bell pepper, arborio rice, asparagus, vegetable broth, and vegan parmesan for making Creamy Vegetable Risotto" class="aligncenter wp-image-30954 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Creamy Vegetable Risotto (30 Minutes!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-copy.jpg" data-pin-description="8-ingredient, 30-minute CREAMY Vegetable Risotto! Flavorful, cheesy, SO delicious #vegan #glutenfree #risotto #plantbased #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Creamy Vegetable Risotto (30 Minutes!)" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-copy.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-copy.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-copy-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-copy-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-copy-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-copy-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-copy-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/><span id="more-30950"></span></p>
<p>This <strong>vegan</strong>, <strong>gluten-free</strong>, <strong>oil-free</strong> risotto is made with <strong>8 ingredients</strong> in <strong>30 minutes</strong> from start to finish!</p>
<p>It starts with fresh vegetables sautéed until just tender. We went with bell pepper, broccolini, and asparagus, but go with whatever is available and in season for you.</p>
<p><iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/6gyATN13W3c" width="680">&amp;amp;amp;lt;span data-mce-type=”bookmark” style=”display: inline-block; width: 0px; overflow: hidden; line-height: 0;” class=”mce_SELRES_start”&amp;amp;amp;gt;﻿&amp;amp;amp;lt;/span&amp;amp;amp;gt;</iframe></p>
<p><img alt="Using a wooden spoon to stir together arborio rice and vegetable broth for this vegan Creamy Vegetable Risotto" class="aligncenter wp-image-30955 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Creamy Vegetable Risotto (30 Minutes!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-3-copy.jpg" data-pin-description="8-ingredient, 30-minute CREAMY Vegetable Risotto! Flavorful, cheesy, SO delicious #vegan #glutenfree #risotto #plantbased #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Creamy Vegetable Risotto (30 Minutes!)" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-3-copy.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-3-copy.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-3-copy-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-3-copy-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-3-copy-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-3-copy-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-3-copy-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>Next, start cooking the risotto by sautéing shallot and then adding arborio rice and white wine for flavor.</p>
<p>Once the wine cooks down, add warmed vegetable broth one ladle at a time and stir as it cooks until “al dente.” Then just add your vegan parmesan cheese and the sautéed vegetables and you’re good to go! It’s that easy.</p>
<p>A few things to keep in mind with risotto:</p>
<ul>
<li>Always use warmed vegetable broth so it doesn’t halt the cooking when added to the rice.</li>
<li>Stir frequently as the rice cooks to prevent sticking.</li>
<li>Cook the rice at a simmer instead of a boil so the rice can cook slowly and evenly.</li>
<li>Cook until just “al dente” to avoid gummy risotto.</li>
</ul>
<p><img alt="Saute pan filled with Creamy Vegetable Risotto" class="aligncenter wp-image-30940 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Creamy Vegetable Risotto (30 Minutes!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-6.jpg" data-pin-description="8-ingredient, 30-minute CREAMY Vegetable Risotto! Flavorful, cheesy, SO delicious #vegan #glutenfree #risotto #plantbased #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Creamy Vegetable Risotto (30 Minutes!)" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-6.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-6.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-6-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-6-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-6-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-6-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/10-ingred-30-minute-CREAMY-Vegetable-Risotto-Flavorful-22cheesy22-SO-delicious-vegan-glutenfree-risotto-plantbased-minimalistbaker-6-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>We hope you all LOVE this dish. It’s:</p>
<p>Creamy<br/>
“Cheesy”<br/>
Flavorful<br/>
Loaded with fresh vegetables<br/>
Easy to make<br/>
&amp; So delicious</p>
<p>This would make the perfect weeknight meal when you need something that’s incredibly satisfying and comforting in a hurry. It would make a delicious entrée or side dish, and it would also work well for dinner parties, as it’s a versatile side dish that complements just about any main.</p>
<p>If you’re into rice dishes, also be sure to check out our <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/easy-vegan-fried-rice/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Vegan Fried Rice</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/mushroom-and-leek-risotto/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Mushroom &amp; Leek Risotto</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/30-minute-cauliflower-rice-stir-fry/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">30-Minute Cauliflower “Rice” Stir Fry</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/cheesy-cauliflower-rice-broccoli-bake/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Cheesy Cauliflower Rice &amp; Broccoli Bake</a>, and <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/veggie-brown-rice-sushi/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Veggie Brown Rice Sushi</a>.</p>
<p>If you try this recipe, let us know! Leave a comment, rate it, and don’t forget to tag a photo <a href="https://www.instagram.com/minimalistbaker/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">#minimalistbaker</a> on Instagram. Cheers, friends!</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name">Creamy Vegetable Risotto (30 minutes!)</h2>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary">
		A healthier take on risotto without oil or butter, replacing cheese with vegan parmesan cheese. Includes plenty of fresh vegetables for fiber and nutrients. An easy 30-minute, 8-ingredient recipe perfect as an entrée or a side.	</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-author-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-author-name">Author:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author">Minimalist Baker</span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-times-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-name">Prep Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time wprm-recipe-prep_time-minutes">5</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time-unit wprm-recipe-prep_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-name">Cook Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time wprm-recipe-cook_time-minutes">25</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time-unit wprm-recipe-cook_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-total-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-total-time-name">Total Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time wprm-recipe-total_time-minutes">30</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time-unit wprm-recipe-total_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-servings-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-servings-name">Servings:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-servings">4</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-servings-unit"></span>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-course-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-course-name">Category:</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-course">
					Entree, Side				</span>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-cuisine-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-cuisine-name">Cuisine:</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-cuisine">
					Gluten-Free, Italian-Inspired, Vegan				</span>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-freezer-friendly-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-freezer-friendly-name">Freezer Friendly</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-freezer-friendly">
					No				</span>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-does-it-keep-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-does-it-keep-name">Does it keep?</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-does-it-keep">
					2-3 Days				</span>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Ingredients</h3>
<div class="wprm-unit-conversion-container"><a class="wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active" data-recipe="34148" data-system="1" href="#">US Customary</a> - <a class="wprm-unit-conversion" data-recipe="34148" data-system="2" href="#">Metric</a></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">RISOTTO</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3 1/2 - 4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cups</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/easy-1-pot-vegetable-broth/" target="_blank">vegetable broth</a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(warmed on the stovetop // store-bought)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">water</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or oil), divided</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">small</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">bundle asparagus</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(ends trimmed or 1 small bundle broccolini, stalks trimmed (we used both))</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">medium</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">red bell pepper</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(seeds + stem removed, thinly sliced)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">~1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">each sea salt and black pepper</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">thinly sliced shallot</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">arborio rice</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">dry white wine</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub more vegetable broth)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/how-to-make-vegan-parmesan-cheese/" target="_blank">vegan parmesan cheese</a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(plus more for serving)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">FOR SERVING optional</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Fresh chopped parsley</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Instructions</h3>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">In a medium saucepan, heat vegetable broth over medium heat. Once simmering, reduce heat to low to keep warm.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>In the meantime, heat a large pan over medium heat. Once hot, add half of the water (or oil) and the asparagus (and/or broccolini) and the red bell pepper. Season with a pinch each salt and pepper and sauté until just tender and slightly browned - 3-4 minutes - stirring frequently. Cover to steam and speed cooking time. Remove from pan, uncover, and set aside.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Heat another large rimmed pan over medium heat. Once hot, add remaining water (or oil) and shallot. Sauté for 1-2 minutes or until softened and very slightly browned.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Add arborio rice and cook for 1 minute, stirring occasionally. Then add dry white wine (or more vegetable broth) and stir gently. Cook for 1-2 minutes or until the liquid is absorbed.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Using a ladle, add warmed vegetable broth 1/2 cup (120 ml) at a time, stirring almost constantly, giving the risotto little breaks to come back to a simmer. The heat should be medium, and there should always be a slight simmer. You want the mixture to be cooking but not boiling or it will get gummy and cook too fast.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Continue to add vegetable broth 1 ladle at a time, stirring to incorporate, until the rice is "al dente" - cooked through but not mushy. This whole process should only take 15-20 minutes (may take longer if making a larger batch).</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Once the rice is cooked through and al dente, remove from heat and season with salt and pepper to taste. Also add vegan parmesan cheese and most of the cooked vegetables, reserving a few for serving. Stir to coat (see photo).</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Taste and adjust flavor as needed, adding a pinch of salt and pepper to taste or more vegan parmesan to enhance the cheesiness.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">To serve, divide between serving bowls and top with remaining vegetables, additional vegan parmesan cheese, and a sprinkle of parsley (optional).</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Best when fresh, though leftovers will keep covered in the refrigerator for 2-3 days. We haven't tried freezing this recipe.</p></div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/?t=1582408114#comment-854780">January 9, 2020 at 5:43 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This recipe is amazing!  I didn’t like the rice al dente so I covered it at the end for about 5-10 minutes. I also used vegan field roast cheese slices and used this time to let it melt in to the rice. So so good! Definitely give this recipe a try.</p>
</div>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-821439">
<article id="article-comment-821439">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for kazy" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/b1c033e1a8fa3f266cd6925d687c5f92?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/b1c033e1a8fa3f266cd6925d687c5f92?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for kazy" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">kazy</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/?t=1582408114#comment-821439">August 19, 2019 at 11:43 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This came out wonderful although I didn’t follow the directions exactly. I used Martha Stewart’s version of cooking the arborio rice. I sauteed the vegetables as instructed in a large  pan but I sauteed the shallots in a large pot rather than another wide rimmed pan, because I only had one large enough pan to accommodate all those vegetables and didn’t have another one for the rice. So I just cooked the rice like I normally would cook rice. Saved me so much time, and it still came out creamy. I sauteed the shallots as instructed but then poured 3 cups of mushroom broth, instead of vegetable broth, in the pan with the shallots, brought it to a boil, stirred once, covered it and let it sit for 20 minutes. So much easier than the incremental multi step process. Once it was done I just poured the whole thing into the vegetable skillet and mixed it all up. I didn’t do any of that reserving the vegetables and adding it on later. I also added more vegetables, like mushrooms, spinach, green peas, I deleted the bell pepper. I also added garlic. And I used real Parmesan cheese. Sprinkled with some parsley and added a bit of lemon juice. I thought it could have used more asparagus, like a pound’s worth, which, when when I make it again I will do. All in all it came out great. Definite keeper. Thanx for the recipe, Dana</p>
<div class="wprm-comment-rating">

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/?t=1582408114#comment-864608">February 19, 2020 at 12:15 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Love this recipe, simple and delicious. I’ve made it quite a few time with all sorts of different veggies and to make it more flavorful without the vegan cheese, I add in garlic with the onions/shallots, and add a little turmeric, ginger, and cayenne to give it some spice.</p>

<img alt="Avatar for Macaela" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fbc29d32c041e127d640224ad0162220?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fbc29d32c041e127d640224ad0162220?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Macaela" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Macaela</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/?t=1582408114#comment-785212">February 9, 2019 at 7:40 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was my first attempt at risotto &amp; was a family favorite! I subbed green beans for asparagus. Also I have tried a number of veggie broth options- my favorite is the Orrington Farms Vegan Broth base where you mix 2 tsp powder for each cup of water- it is favorful like chicken broth, but plant based. I also recommend using more than 4c broth for a creamy version!</p>
</div>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/?t=1582408114#comment-779853">December 30, 2018 at 3:11 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Delicious! My husband, who is vegetarian, and I (who is not) both really enjoyed this dish. I added spinach to the vegetable mix, as I had a tub that needed to get eaten, in addition to the asparagus and peppers. The asparagus gave it a nice fresh crunch (and I love asparagus!), and the spinach added some extra green veges to the recipe, which is much appreciated after the decadence of Christmas! I used regular Parmesan, as neither of us are vegan, and it was delicious! Simple to make and a tasty change from pasta or other rice dishes (I’m not a very good vegetarian cook – I find it quite challenging). Thanks for the recipe!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>I adapted this into a paella style dish with mushrooms and cannellini beans too, stir fried everything in a paella pan, added the broth all at once, brought it to a boil, then let it sit and simmer for 20 min. No stirring required, and it turned out great!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made this recipe today and it was delicious!  I used both asparagus and broccoli, and Parmesan cheese. I t was great! next time I will add mushrooms. However, the 5 minute prep time was longer than that. I guess I’m not such a quick chopper. There is no way I can chop/slice vegetables that quick, and the cook time was longer too. Overall, probably at least 45 minutes. But definitely worth it!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Love it and so does everyone that has tried this. I sub in sweet onion for shallots. First time I made with broccoli and red pepper, used vegan “not-chicken” bouillon cubes for veg broth. Second time, I made baby bella mushrooms, peas and peppers (the peppers were completely unnecessary), I used vegan “not beef’ bouillon for veg broth.  Each was really, really good.  Made both oil free. Great recipe and for some reason, it’s fun to cook.  Thanks!!</p>

<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Francesca" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d4f1cc9b82d9120d73e3c16cbea79401?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d4f1cc9b82d9120d73e3c16cbea79401?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Francesca" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Francesca</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/?t=1582408114#comment-747998">March 29, 2018 at 1:27 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Very good adaptation of traditional risotto, If I can add something, for who is up to using olive oil/vegan butter, the ‘soffritto’ with shallots (or onions) super finely chopped at the beginning + olive oil and / or vegan butter is one of the most important thing in making a real risotto. Also leave it rest (italian ‘mantecare’) for some minutes at the end, covered after having added some olive oil/vegan butter. </p>
<p>I have to say best vegan risotto is with porcini mushrooms and butternut squash (the only one that makes me forget there is no real parmigiano!) </p>
<p>Francesca</p>
</div>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/?t=1582408114#comment-749163">April 9, 2018 at 9:38 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Peas and Mushrooms are wonderful in this recipe: The second time I made this dish, I used baby Bella mushrooms, peas and yellow/orange pepper. The pepper was not needed and the peas and ‘shrooms worked REALLY well. I don’t like veg broth (even homemade), so I use Vegan bouillon (Not Beed Cubes for the Mushroom and Pea version) and it was amazing. I made a large batch and took some to my neighbors and they loved it as well!</p>

<li class="comment odd alt depth-2" id="comment-747952">
<article id="article-comment-747952">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for G" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/b4ccb23edbe5fb5371a27ce2a6f863ab?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/b4ccb23edbe5fb5371a27ce2a6f863ab?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for G" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">G</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/creamy-vegetable-risotto-30-minutes/?t=1582408114#comment-747952">March 28, 2018 at 12:23 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Arborio rice is the classic rice for risotto because it is starchier than other rice and creates the creamy texture of the dish. If you use already cooked brown rice your dish would not be risotto and would not taste the same as this recipe. You’d essentially just have rice and vegetables, which is good, but not risotto.</p>
</div>
<div class="comment-reply"><a aria-label="Reply to G" class="comment-reply-link" data-belowelement="comment-747952" data-commentid="747952" data-postid="30950" data-respondelement="respond" href="#comment-747952" rel="nofollow">Reply</a></div>
